-                Download current and past regulatory reports for Facebook and Instagram.
-              </p></a></div></div></div><div class="_9z0o"><div class="_9nv8" id="u_0_b_UE"><div class="_9nv9"><div class="_9nva"></div><div class="_9nvc"></div><div class="_9nvb"></div></div></div></div></div><section class="_9ntw _9ntz _9nt-"><div class="_9nu3"><div class="_9nrh"><div class="_9nxk _9ocs _9od0"><div class="_9nxl"><div class="_9nxn"><a href="/" class="_9nrc _9noc _9noa _9qfr _9ny2 _9t0u"><span class="_9nxm _97fe">Home</span></a><img class="_9nxo img" alt="Arrow Right" src="https://static.xx.fbcdn.net/rsrc.php/yX/r/OPwWf9DfGY-.svg" width="16" height="16" /></div><div class="_9nxn"><a href="/policies" class="_9nrc _9noc _9noa _9qfr _9ny2 _9t0u"><span class="_9nxm _97fe">Policies</span></a><img class="_9nxo img" alt="Arrow Right" src="https://static.xx.fbcdn.net/rsrc.php/yX/r/OPwWf9DfGY-.svg" width="16" height="16" /></div></div><div class="_9nnu _9ny0 _9nxp"></div></div><div class="_9nri"><h1 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9nn7 _9nmw _9qfj _9qfh _9no_">Facebook Community Standards</h1></div></div><div class="_9nrg"><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nor _9qfr _9nob _9no_">The Facebook Community Standards outline what is and isn&#039;t allowed on Facebook.</p></div></div></section><section class="_9ntw _9nty _9nu2"><div class="_9nu3"><div class="_9nrg"><h3 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9nmy _9qfl _9qfh _9nos">Introduction</h3><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9qfr _9nob _9nos">Every day, people use Facebook to share their experiences, connect with friends and family, and build communities. It’s a service for more than 2 billion people to freely express themselves across countries and cultures and in dozens of languages.</p><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9qfr _9nob _9nos">Meta recognizes how important it is for Facebook to be a place where people feel empowered to communicate, and we take our role seriously in keeping abuse off the service. That’s why we developed standards for what is and isn’t allowed on Facebook.</p><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nor _9qfr _9nob _9nos">These standards are based on feedback from people and the advice of experts in fields like technology, public safety and human rights. To ensure everyone’s voice is valued, we take great care to create standards that include different views and beliefs, especially from people and communities that might otherwise be overlooked or marginalized.</p><br /><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nor _9qfr _9nob _9nos"><b>Please note that the US English version of the Community Standards reflects the most up to date set of the policies and should be used as the primary document.</b></p><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9qfs _9nob _9nos"><iframe src="https://www.facebook.com/cms/video/?id=850337606335586&amp;height=360&amp;width=640&amp;loop=0&amp;ext=1716926582&amp;hash=AcrqxIFripstd-Y6eyk" allowfullscreen="1" height="360" width="640" scrolling="no" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" frameborder="0"></iframe></p></div></div></section><section class="_9ntw _9nu2"><div class="_9nu3"><div class="_9nnu _9nn_ _9nnv"></div><div class="_9nrg"><h3 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9nmy _9qfl _9qfh _9nos">Our commitment to voice</h3><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nor _9qfr _9nob _9nos">The goal of our Community Standards is to create a place for expression and give people a voice. Meta wants people to be able to talk openly about the issues that matter to them, whether through written comments, photos, music, or other artistic mediums, even if some may disagree or find them objectionable. In some cases, we allow content—which would otherwise go against our standards—if it’s <a href="https://transparency.fb.com/features/approach-to-newsworthy-content/" target="_blank" data-lnfb-mode="ie">newsworthy</a> and in the public interest. We do this only after weighing the public interest value against the risk of harm, and we look to international human rights standards to make these judgments. In other cases, we may remove content that uses ambiguous or implicit language when additional context allows us to reasonably understand that the content goes against our standards.</p><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9non _9qfr _9nob _9nos">Our commitment to expression is paramount, but we recognize the internet creates new and increased opportunities for abuse. For these reasons, when we limit expression, we do it in service of one or more of the following values:</p></div></div></section><section class="_9ntw _9nu2"><div class="_9nu3"><div id="u_0_c_Vx"><div class="_9nsk _9ns- _9nt6 _9ntm" id="u_0_d_DZ"><div class="_9nrf"><div class="_9ntv"><img class="img" alt="" src="https://scontent-sjc3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.8562-6/136893606_849918935579882_213472362566516880_n.jpg?_nc_cat=1&amp;ccb=1-7&amp;_nc_sid=f537c7&amp;_nc_ohc=StuSLzMnYqgQ7kNvgFVK7BU&amp;_nc_ht=scontent-sjc3-1.xx&amp;oh=00_AYCxm3PDhFtXKAHCbbuF2wIBL8DQj6tp7O37gZITxjA-vg&amp;oe=665C16CF" id="u_0_e_Z8" /></div><h2 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9o40 _9nn1 _9nmx _9qfq _9oxt _9nos">AUTHENTICITY</h2><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nol _9qfr _9nob _9nos">We want to make sure the content people see on Facebook is authentic. We believe that authenticity creates a better environment for sharing, and that’s why we don’t want people using Facebook to misrepresent who they are or what they’re doing.</p></div></div><div class="_9nsk _9ns- _9nt6 _9ntm" id="u_0_f_uC"><div class="_9nrf"><div class="_9ntv"><img class="img" alt="" src="https://scontent-sjc3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.8562-6/137256059_2800543870233431_455035967167740410_n.jpg?_nc_cat=1&amp;ccb=1-7&amp;_nc_sid=f537c7&amp;_nc_ohc=6yeQ9jg2N-IQ7kNvgH-Ph3H&amp;_nc_ht=scontent-sjc3-1.xx&amp;oh=00_AYB1fYK-shp7VCzTCRyiSowSqpGULABFlIvLsX31E63eXA&amp;oe=665C0E3E" id="u_0_g_E/" /></div><h2 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9o40 _9nn1 _9nmx _9qfq _9oxt _9nos">SAFETY</h2><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nol _9qfr _9nob _9nos">We’re committed to making Facebook a safe place. We remove content that could contribute to a risk of harm to the physical security of persons. Content that threatens people has the potential to intimidate, exclude or silence others and isn’t allowed on Facebook.</p></div></div></div><div id="u_0_h_HK"><div class="_9nsk _9ns- _9nt6 _9ntm" id="u_0_i_Tr"><div class="_9nrf"><div class="_9ntv"><img class="img" alt="" src="https://scontent-sjc3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.8562-6/137145103_308994903869841_4708570808613729754_n.jpg?_nc_cat=108&amp;ccb=1-7&amp;_nc_sid=f537c7&amp;_nc_ohc=0GQP57MZ2hkQ7kNvgHvThJa&amp;_nc_ht=scontent-sjc3-1.xx&amp;oh=00_AYD1zB2o7zfn-ye1rpNZAi9UqWodYtvVxxdtURZbpfKhKA&amp;oe=665BFFCC" id="u_0_j_Zw" /></div><h2 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9o40 _9nn1 _9nmx _9qfq _9oxt _9nos">PRIVACY</h2><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nol _9qfr _9nob _9nos">We’re committed to protecting personal privacy and information. Privacy gives people the freedom to be themselves, choose how and when to share on Facebook and connect more easily.</p></div></div><div class="_9nsk _9ns- _9nt6 _9ntm" id="u_0_k_0r"><div class="_9nrf"><div class="_9ntv"><img class="img" alt="" src="https://scontent-sjc3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.8562-6/137151366_203760844736656_1882032595123025998_n.jpg?_nc_cat=1&amp;ccb=1-7&amp;_nc_sid=f537c7&amp;_nc_ohc=8_JIv9N1Uk0Q7kNvgE-GIQ0&amp;_nc_ht=scontent-sjc3-1.xx&amp;oh=00_AYAhthdoLVG_5YjYCcVUdawZSqinDOzs_jgxFRbPizGqwA&amp;oe=665C120B" id="u_0_l_p2" /></div><h2 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9o40 _9nn1 _9nmx _9qfq _9oxt _9nos">DIGNITY</h2><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nol _9qfr _9nob _9nos">We believe that all people are equal in dignity and rights. We expect that people will respect the dignity of others and not harass or degrade others.</p></div></div></div><div class="_9nnu _9nn_ _9nnv"></div></div></section><section class="_9ntw _9ntz _9nu2"><div class="_9nu3"><div id="u_0_m_lJ"><div class="_9nsk _9ns- _9nt6 _9ntm" id="u_0_n_du"><div class="_9nrf"><h3 class="_9nmv _9nsb _9nn7 _9nmy _9qfl _9qfh _9nos">Community Standards</h3><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nok _9qfr _9nob _9nos">Our Community Standards apply to everyone, all around the world, and to all types of content, including AI-generated content.</p><p class="_9qmn _9nod _9nok _9qfr _9nob _9nos">Each section of our Community Standards starts with a “Policy Rationale” that sets out the aims of the policy followed by specific policy lines that outline: </p><p class="_9qmn
